#I am grateful to SirUmnei, VulpesDolosus and Exotek for their teachings on creating custom class mods ("COMs").

#COM manufacturers are altered through Gibbed.
#Do not execute this file in conjunction with SirUmnei's 'COMOverhaulPack" file.
#It is highly recommended that you take SirUmnei's 'Presentation List Overrides' from the aforementioned 'COMOverhaulPack' file, copypaste and save them as their own file, and execute that file AFTER this one.
#Execute this file and the 'Presentation List Overrides' file described above as late as possible.
#The Borderlands 2 GitHub and Shadow's Evil Hideout on Discord are the only authorized locations for downloading my COMs.
#These COMs were designed and balance at Overpowered Level 8 (i.e. OP8); and with theNocturni's "UVHM+" series of mods in mind.
#You must execute this file before entering a game. Otherwise, Sanity Check will delete all of the TTaoDK COMs within this file.

#Legacine's Legendary Custom Class Mods
